# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
When using vectors with kinematics we can still use the following SUVAT formula ^ZkqiYQDS

If a particle starts from the point with position vector r  and moves with constant velocity v, then its displacement from its initial position at time t is vt and its position vector r is given by r = r  + vt ^zUnYrmXR

0 ^ucHeyCAC

0 ^Y23tuoHf

position vector = vector from orogin ^6pn4mjQ9

A particle P move with constant acceleration. At time t = 0, P is moving in the direction (4i + 3j) with speed 15m/s. 6 seconds later P is moving with velocity (-12i + 6j)m/s
Find the acceleration of P. ^CV8O9TlJ

A particle P moves in a straight line with constant velocity. Initially P is at the point A with position vector (4i-3j)m. At time t = 3, P is at the point B with position vector (-5i+9j)m
a) Find the velocity of P
When t = 5, P is at the point C
b) Find the distance AC ^no2Y9BWK

Equate the i's and equate the j's the time should be the same ^bOA1r8fV
